<Rate>4< /Rate><text>I came here purposely to try out the Amaretti cookies. My sister LOVES these type of cookies and there were reviews on Yelp that they make them here. I came here and  bought 5 of them ($1 a piece - a bit pricey for the size of the cookie) and 2 wedding cookies. They did have sandwiches too that looked appealing but I did not get any at this time. <Time>1472514098670< /Time><rating>5</rating>< Review>
Easily the Best cannoli in town! These guys not only make their own cannoli shells but the ricotta cream filling is this ultra tasty, whipped to perfection cream that you just can't stop eating. All the other sweet treats are no less impressive. Many types of cookies and all of them fresh and uncompromisingly delicious. Definitely try the macaroons and the chocolate dipped cookies.
On the sandwich side they make spectacular subs, mostly with traditional Italian ingredients, some of them toasted. I just had the eggplants and mozzarella sammy and it's an instant favorite.
There is some outside seating, so you can enjoy your lunch/dessert without delay.
A great contribution to the neighborhood.< /Review>

< Review>
Used to be a great local business with friendly and knowledgeable staff. It have gone downhill considerably with terrible customer service and monopolistic practices.

This company sources most of their products through MoreFlavor Ltd, who sources grain, hops and other basic supplies through a national supplier. Basic grains, hops and general supplies direct from MoreFlavor is 30%+ less then Brewmeisters. The markup Brewmeister applies on 'specialty' gains is well in excess of 100% and MoreBeer is located within an hour of the greater Sacramento area, where Brewmeister operates. As an example, a 50lb sack of grain costs $30 through MoreBeer, $50 through Brewmeister.

You are much better off using any of the available online competition for your homebrew needs and won't have to deal with one of their rude employees.<//Review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
One of the rare occassions where I've had no complaints about an establishment whatsoever. The moment you walk in, the Hispanic culture that is the atmosphere grabs you and pulls you in, making you feel at home. The mood of the entire room is inviting you further and further as their art and food reels you into your seat. The service is top notch, and makes you feel as if they are delighted that you're eating there. The chips and salsa alone were almost enough to make me full, they were so fresh and delicious. Finally, my meal. The chicken, the rice, the veggies, were all so masterfully prepared on my dish that I felt that I was judging some sort of top chef competition. The taste was of everything was so perfect that I kept wanting more and more, and more, so much so I felt that I should just order an entirely new one for leftovers. This is absolutely one of the best restaurants available, anywhere.<//Text>

112540002531229988315< /user_id>
< Text>
What a dump. I took a friend for lunch on a Sunday afternoon. We walked into a crowded-feeling room that felt chaotic & unclean, with big-screen TVs visually screaming -- and at least one "actually" screaming -- on every wall in the place, not just in the bar. The booths were cramped. We both ordered flautas -- just an appetizer -- hers with grilled chicken & mine with carnitas, which wasn't on the menu but which they were able to accommodate. But they were dry & there wasn't enough topping; I had to buy an extra side of guacamole. We also each got a side of beans (didn't come with the meal, so paid extra) and a soda (THREE bucks each & we were not offered a refill). For this I paid 40 bucks, plus a tip. I couldn't believe it. Almost 50 dollars for dry flautas, 12 cents' worth of beans, and a couple of cokes in a seedy-feeling, noisy room. I'm still in shock. I'll NEVER go there again. Oh, & add another dollar sign to the two up there next to the restaurant name. I grew up in Southern California & have been eating Mexican food since I could eat solid food, & have had plenty of the real thing thanks to many Mexican friends whose moms are outstanding cooks, & I can tell you, this place wasn't even close. I've had way better Mexican food from little out-of-the-way places & street vendors. I'm going to miss that 50 bucks until the day I die. One of the worst dining experiences I've ever had. DON'T WASTE YOUR MONEY.</Text>

< Text>
Two kids, three adults for lunch was $86, $100 with tip. I ordered a southwestern salad with chicken. Good thing I added chicken otherwise it would have been the most expensive lettuce I ever bought. Aside from the chicken add on, it had three slices of cucumber, three slices of tomato, some tortilla strips and little cheese. At $15, way overpriced. Guacamole was $9 and FULL of tomatoes. Anyone who loves guac knows that's the Cardinal sin. Because of the overload of tomatoes it was runnier than it should have been and lacked flavor. Son's chicken taco was dry as a bone. Both son's said the beens and rice were good. The other two adults I was with ordered burritos. The carnitas was dry. The chili verde was good. Server was good but rushed. Slow down when you approach your tables, run when you're not at the tables. Decor was nice. They have a serve yourself salsa bar. Not a fan as I feel it's one less thing they need to serve you so really your doing their job. I'm not sitting in a restaurant to keep getting up to serve myself, especially at this price. Won't be going back. BTW, in my career I've been the purchasing manager for foodservice distributors so I know how much food costs are, also managed restaurants in high school and while going to college, and for what you get, not pleased.</Text>

< review>
Almost perfect. If you love mexican food as much as you should, this place is for you. The bar is as well run as any I've ever seen. The tamales and rellenos are perfection. the salsa bar has plenty of choices. the wait staff are very good and fast enough. They have been overrun with too many customers at one time but our food still came out hot and on time. We learned to go here super late afternoon, when they were not ultra busy. TVs are not too loud (I like that). Prices are spot on. Just where you expect them to be for top quality food and service. Bar prices are good too. If I could change one thing here it would be to remove the wall of crosses. You will see what I mean when you get there. Not needed. The rest of the decorations are great. You can tell they spent GOOD money on the remodel. Hacienda is very clean with a big city feel and a small town charm. Enjoy.</review>

<rate>4< /rate>< text>
Great location, friendly staff, and pet-friendly! I wish their food was better so that I could give it 5 stars... at least they give you unlimited tortilla chips & salsa.  I had chosen this place on the fact alone that they offer a doggy-patio. I ordered the combo plate with a cheese enchilada, which was delicious... hard to screw up... along with a carne asada taco. The rice and black beans were perfect but the carne asada in the taco was so bland and overcooked, I couldn't enjoy my full meal. Something didn't sit right with me either because I had to use the restroom soon afterwards... as well as my husband :/ I will try this place again when I come to visit Big Bear again but I will definitely NOT order anything with carne asada.< /text>

< review>
Most of the food was good or great. Unfortunately what I ordered was just bad. The service here was horrible. Some of the staff did a good job, others were just inexcusably unprofessional. We arrived with a large party of 15 people on a Wednesday. I understand that this can overwhelm the staff and we were all willing to cut them some serious slack. Unfortunately it quickly became apparent that no amount of slack would be sufficient. We were at our tables for 25 minutes before drink orders were taken. Refills were haphazard and communication was horrible. I had to go hunting through the restaurant to discover there was a salsa bar. The salsa was amazing. When the initial wave of food showed up after 80 minutes it was delicious. I got to sample the food of everyone around me because, inexplicably, my tortilla soup didn't arrive until everyone had finished their meals. Five of us ordered the tortilla soup and when it finally arrived it looked like I was in for a really good meal. I was dumbfounded to find that it was bland and entirely lacking in character. Everyone who ordered the soup agreed and didn't eat it. Someone messed up on the soup. That is the only explanation. I brought this to the attention of the server and made sure to tell him that the rest of the food was great. I suggested that we really shouldn't pay for it. He gave me a slack jaw look and found an excuse to talk to someone else. When I pressed the point he argued with me about that I said it was ok. I still don't know what the heck he was smoking there. When he finally split the checks (more arguing there) he only took off my soup and left the other 4 on. I was so angry my family refused to let me make a big deal about it. They all told me to write a review instead. There was plenty of additional drama and by the time it was over we all had a very bad taste in our mouth. Ironically not from the food. If you go to this restaurant please don't be silent. They are on the verge of being great. They just need to train their staff about basic restaurant practices and nothing will change unless you speak up.< /review>
